<rate>1</rate>< Text>
The food itself is okay, if you like Korean style chicken and alternate takes on pizza.  The service is downright terrible.

When I went there on a group outing, we ordered separately and to go, due to differing schedules that would force some people to leave at different times.  It still should have been a simple enough affair, since we had over an hour free.

Despite my order being an earlier one, others in my group got their food far before mine.  I waited over an hour, periodically asking about my order and being reassured that my order was coming.  People who ordered after me yet received their food before me had sat down to munch while accompanying me.

Then I was told that they forgot to do my order.  The rest of my group had already finished their food, and it was almost time for the group to head back.  The waitress and manager offered a very anemic apology, seeming to believe a free bottle of cheap soda would suffice for a wait of more than an hour for no good reason.  This is with knowing that it make me waste even more time waiting for food they hadn't even started making.

I demanded a refund.  They went through a big production of having trouble reversing my credit card charges.  I made sure to also keep pestering for a copy of the reversed charges, to ensure I had a record of what happened, and to see the original signed receipt, so that I could cross out my signature and void it.  It took them so long just to understand why I would want to do so.

Through all this, the apologies, both about the food and about the refund, always came with a claimed caveat that it wasn't that person's fault.  No one was willing to take responsibility.

If you like the food at Love Letter, go to a different branch.  The one in Chino Hills will likely leave you disappointed at best, angry at worst.<//Text>

The food is as expected. A Korean styled pizza (nothing like what we know pizza ) and mildly salted fried chicken. Again it's all about Korean style.

To be Frank, OVERLY PRICED! Spent approx 45$ on a cheap quality pizza (like one of those 5$ pizza) and a whole chicken fried!

By the way, they charged my bill (which still pending due to discrepancy) without my signature.

The worst of the evening caos, after seeing the manager? Kenny? coming out of the kitchen with FLOUR all over his bare HANDS and trying to resolve their order mistake at the counter,  I am DEFINITELY NOT going back.  Let's hope the white floury powder on his hands is not from the pizza dough he was making in the back. Instead I am praying it is from the gloves... puke.to think..!

I was anticipating so much for its opening in CH yet this being the secind time giving it a try.... FAIL!! I rather spend 45$ at Buffalo place or WingStop.

The service is sloooow and the good does come out slow.  It does take time to fry.

Their marketing of all natural vegetable seasoning...  really? All natural?  Hmmmm...<//Text>

< Text>
Little biased on this one since it has been my main taco shop growing up. Hidden in Paradise Hills, this is little staple has stood the test of time. The decor from when I was in middle still holds strong nearly 15 years later. Even the Shakira cut out behind the register remains unmoved, her powerful eyes looking over the store. Outside of its nostalgia, is a basic taco shop with all the traditional fares. To be honest, their fries are soggy, tortilla too stale, and sauces are bland. However, decently seasoned meat, solid portions, and $7.95 carne asada fries make it my taco shop. It may not be special for anyone else trying it out, but if I'm in the area and am craving it, Ill swing by every time.<//Text>

< user_id>
112575396580815519209<//user_id>
<name>Hannah Coda<//name>< time>
1622924456714< /time>
<rating>2<//rating>< review>
The decor inside was really cool. The music was loud (maybe it was so that when it was really busy it would be backround music. But it was just us 2 and we couldn't hear each other speak.

They do take your card before you order and hold it the entire time.

I couldn't decide what to get so I eventually just decided on chicken tenders, so I wasn't expecting much. But the waitress said "ooh, good choice!" So that got my hopes up. They turned out to be the worst chicken tenders from a Mexican restaurant that I've ever had. So dry and pretty sure they were burned.

My husband's brunch meal looked good and was super big though.

If I ever come back, I'll go to the other restaurant by the beach.</review>

< Text>
PLEASE! Read your RECEIPT!!

This is coming from a customer who has been to this and MANY Cabo Cantina's and I believe they are trained to skim (not scam) the customers.

They literally take your order with a smile, then serve you whatever drink they want. OR They serve you what you order and add El DORADO to the bill. El Dorado is the premium drink that is $12.95 or $13.95 depending on how they decide to bill it (or their fancy keying or renaming it to another, cheaper drink). I ALWAYS order the TJ classic which is $7.95 and the most basic Jose Cuervo Margarita.

They will charge for the El Dorado (Patron tequila) margarita and say they made a mistake if you challenge it. Then, instead of changing that, they offer to remove a food item (for alcohol billing and for skimming purposes) instead of adjusting the real price of the drinks you ORDERED.  They will say the price difference (b/c its not listed on the menu) is only $1 or $2 but as you can see, its $5 or $6!

In the End, ALWAYS check your receipt.  Do NOT pay for drinks misattributed to your bill. And, do NOT let them take advantage of you, because as long as I have been going there, THEY WILL ALWAYS TRY!.

I have been going there for over 11 years, and Everytime, EVERY location, they try the same skim (scam) and everytime I catch them, call them out, and get my bill adjusted!

Do the SAME!<//Text>

< Review>
If you are looking for a place to drink next to the beach with less than ridiculous pricing, than this is a decent option. Well, pretty good considering it's one of only a few options.

Their margaritas are insanely sweet, even the classic. Also, please note that pricing on drinks can be a bit deceptive, especially during happy hour.

Food on the other hand is surprisingly good. Flavorful and in pretty generous portions, this is definitely not a good place for a diet but great with a beer or two.

Service is pretty unresponsive, so it isn't a great place if you're in a rush. But if you're afternoon or evening is relaxed, it's not a bad place to spend some time.</Review>

< Text>
Extremely racist! We came in with a group of college educated, professional people after a HBCU event and the manager immediately got concerned. He walked over to us as we were walking in and said, "we don't want any loud noise in here." "What?", I thought in my head. What insinuated that we were going to be loud? Yet as soon as we walked in we were asked or told not to be loud. We hadn't even taken our seats yet. As the time went on we were met with extremely poor service. The waitress took 15-20 mins before she ever arrived to our table, got our orders incorrect and demanded that we pay first. It's our policy she exclaimed. Not true by they way. Our food never came out and the manager kept walking by watching everything we were doing. One my friends heard something funny and busted out laughing and slapped the table in a big chuckle. <name>Elizabeth Trejo<//name>< Date>
1415834348696</Date>
<Rate>4</Rate>< review>
For several years now I've been coming to this Cabo Cantina every so often. Mostly to watch sports and have some of their giant margaritas. I finally went to their Taco Tuesday and I was very impressed!

I've never liked their food much (I'm Mexican, I know what authentic Mexican food should taste like), but the margaritas are great along with other drinks. The decor and atmosphere is very fun and young. They have an upstairs and downstairs area, both with outside patios. Located right off the Venice Beach Boardwalk, it is the perfect location for "drinks on the beach" (you can't literally drink on the beach, unfortunately, but you catch my flow).

Taco Tuesday was great! I was worried about trying the tacos but once they were on the table I was excited to try them! Not disapointed at all; they were really delicious, at least the steak and chicken ones I had were. They had plenty of meat and came with a side of mexican rice and black beans. Paired up with a giant margarita, Taco Tuesday was perfect here! It was a full house for the Happy Hour which goes from 4pm-10pm, everyone enjoying a conversation over sports, food, and drinks.

Since it gets really busy, service isn't as quick but thats understandable. All the servers are very nice. I've never had a issue with customer service here. Parking sucks, but if you are lucky you might just get a meter right outside or there is also valet across the street and a parking lot at the end of the street.</review>

<review>You really can't miss Cabo Cantina when walking on the street here because of the crowd and the general rukus (popular here). I found Cabo to be true to my other Cabo experience in Pacific Beach (party town numero uno). If you like this type of energy then this will be your vehicle of happiness.

Surprisingly the overall ratings are only 3.5. My question is how can a place be this popular, crowded most of the time and get this low of a rating. Perhaps those that enjoy the vibe are not the type to do a review (ever think of that). Sometimes the most demonstrative visitor is someone that may have had an off experience. They almost always give the lowest 1 Star rating; when in general they should expect to have some attitude because of the mix of alcohol and average tolerance to the spirits.

By:
cmilton111

<gmapID>0x80c2ba8e401b2d1d:0x924fbf79ef48be8c</gmapID><Rating>1< /Rating>< Pics>

< text>
I barely write reviews because I dnt wanna take the time to talk about a place unless it really deserves it. I have never been to a place that treats you with such disrespect. This cabo cantina needs to take some pointers from the other locations like the one in West Hollywood.  I get it it's like the "Mexican style" bar and grill so you don't expect much. But you should at least be treated like a customer. First the blended Mega Margarita that I split with my friends was really icy. It taste like a slurpee from 7 11 that was really watered down. Way to much ice. I coulnt even taste the flavor I got let alone the alcohol. But I drank it anyway. Didn't bother to tell the server. We also got nachos which was great. Then I ordered buy one get one Margarita on ice which was really good. The problem didn't really come until we got the bill. The server (I dnt know her name but seems to be a dark hair white girl)  wrote 20% of 100 =$20 on the ticket. I'm a server my friends are servers so we felt really disrespected at the fact that she wrote it on the bill. Like we were going to do it anyway because we are of the industry but she didn't have to write it on the bill. We felt because we are a diverse group of minorities she had a need to write it on the bill. Some restaurants have the percentages PRINTED at the bottom for your convenience, but she flat out wrote it with her pen. When we asked her about it she brushed it off and said it was a bad habit. So then we start to wonder if this is policy so we called a manager( a seemingly white male named Guy )over. Before he came I saw her debrief him of what happen (which was really nothing). When he came he seem to already know what he was gonna say. When we asked him if it's policy he said yes because we have a lot of tourists come here. Then I said tourist are not you shouldn't try to force tip out of pple. Then he said its policy and its not going to change. And then said every cabo cantina is different.  I thought to myself yes every one is different, they aren't racist. The manager NAMED GUY was very rude. When I asked him for his name he said it was Guy and then he asked for mine and I said no. Which seem to really piss him off. It then Looked like he gestured to security to kick us out. They didn't get a chance to we were leaving anyway. My thing is you never know who you are going to get we were going to tip 20% anyway. Because of the manager we tipped her NOTHING. She wasnt a good server anyway. The team is only as good as the leader and the leader sucks. Not coming here again. I'll stick to what I know.</text>

< name>

< text>
I barely write reviews because I dnt wanna take the time to talk about a place unless it really deserves it. I have never been to a place that treats you with such disrespect. This cabo cantina needs to take some pointers from the other locations like the one in West Hollywood.  I get it it's like the "Mexican style" bar and grill so you don't expect much. But you should at least be treated like a customer. First the blended Mega Margarita that I split with my friends was really icy. It taste like a slurpee from 7 11 that was really watered down. Way to much ice. I coulnt even taste the flavor I got let alone the alcohol. But I drank it anyway. Didn't bother to tell the server. We also got nachos which was great. Then I ordered buy one get one Margarita on ice which was really good. The problem didn't really come until we got the bill. The server (I dnt know her name but seems to be a dark hair white girl)  wrote 20% of 100 =$20 on the ticket. I'm a server my friends are servers so we felt really disrespected at the fact that she wrote it on the bill. Like we were going to do it anyway because we are of the industry but she didn't have to write it on the bill. We felt because we are a diverse group of minorities she had a need to write it on the bill. Some restaurants have the percentages PRINTED at the bottom for your convenience, but she flat out wrote it with her pen. When we asked her about it she brushed it off and said it was a bad habit. So then we start to wonder if this is policy so we called a manager( a seemingly white male named Guy )over. Before he came I saw her debrief him of what happen (which was really nothing). When he came he seem to already know what he was gonna say. When we asked him if it's policy he said yes because we have a lot of tourists come here. Then I said tourist are not you shouldn't try to force tip out of pple. Then he said its policy and its not going to change. And then said every cabo cantina is different.  I thought to myself yes every one is different, they aren't racist. The manager NAMED GUY was very rude. When I asked him for his name he said it was Guy and then he asked for mine and I said no. Which seem to really piss him off. It then Looked like he gestured to security to kick us out. They didn't get a chance to we were leaving anyway. My thing is you never know who you are going to get we were going to tip 20% anyway. Because of the manager we tipped her NOTHING. She wasnt a good server anyway. The team is only as good as the leader and the leader sucks. Not coming here again. I'll stick to what I know.</text>
